  var issOpts = {
      fallbackFlag: 1
    , isDigitalFeaturesEnabled: 0
    , isWayfindingEnabled: 0
    , issPrimeEligible: []
    , dropdown: "select.searchSelect"
    , departmentText: "en {department}"
    , suggestionText: "Sugerencias de búsqueda"
    , isTriggerIssOnClick: 0
    , np: 0
    , issCorpus: []
    , cf: 1
  };
  

  if (opts.isUseAuiIss === 1 && window.$Nav) {
    window.$Nav.when('sx.iss').run('iss-mason-init', function(iss){
      var issInitObj = buildIssInitObject(opts, issOpts, true);
      new iss.IssParentCoordinator(issInitObj);

      tryInitClientTriggeredWeblabs(issInitObj);
    });
  } else if (window.$SearchJS) {
    
    var iss;

    // BEGIN Deprecated globals
    var issHost = opts.host
      , issMktid = opts.marketId
      , issSearchAliases = opts.searchAliases
      , updateISSCompletion = function() { iss.updateAutoCompletion(); };
    // END deprecated globals

    
    
    
    $SearchJS.when('jQuery', 'search-js-autocomplete-lib').run('autocomplete-init', initializeAutocomplete);
    $SearchJS.when('canCreateAutocomplete').run('createAutocomplete', createAutocomplete);

    
    if (opts.isDdInT3) {
      $SearchJS.when('search-js-autocomplete').run('autocomplete-dd-init', function(){ mergeBTFDropdown(); });
    }

    if (opts.isDdInT1) {
      $SearchJS.when('search-js-autocomplete').run('autocomplete-dd-init', function(){ searchDropdown(); });
    }

  } // END conditional for window.$SearchJS

  
  
  function initializeAutocomplete(jQuery) {
    
    var issInitObj = buildIssInitObject(opts, issOpts);

    tryInitClientTriggeredWeblabs(issInitObj);
  } // END initializeAutocomplete

  
  
  function tryInitClientTriggeredWeblabs(issInitObj) {
    
    if (opts.isDoCtw) {
      $SearchJS.importEvent('search-csl');
      $SearchJS.when('search-csl').run('autocomplete-csl-init', function delegateToInitSearchCsl(searchCSL) { initSearchCsl( searchCSL, issInitObj ); } );
    } else {
      $SearchJS.declare('canCreateAutocomplete', issInitObj);
    }
  }

  
  
  function initSearchCsl(searchCSL, issInitObject) {
    searchCSL.init(opts.pageType, (window.ue && window.ue.rid) || opts.requestId);

    
    var keydownCtw = opts.keydownTriggeredWeblabs;
    var displayCtw = opts.displayTriggeredWeblabs;

    
    issInitObject.doCTWKeydown = function(e) {
        for (var i = 0; i < keydownCtw.length; i++) {
          searchCSL.addWlt(keydownCtw[i].call ? keydownCtw[i](e) : keydownCtw[i]);
        }
      };

    issInitObject.doCTWDisplay = function(data) {
        for (var i = 0; i < displayCtw.length; i++) {
          searchCSL.addWlt(displayCtw[i].call ? displayCtw[i](data) : displayCtw[i]);
        }
      };

    $SearchJS.declare('canCreateAutocomplete', issInitObject);
  } // END initSearchCsl

  
  
  function createAutocomplete(issObject) {
    iss = new AutoComplete(issObject);

    $SearchJS.publish('search-js-autocomplete', iss);

    logMetrics();
  } // END createAutocomplete

  
  
  function buildIssInitObject(opts, issOpts, isNewIss) {
    var issInitObj = {
        src: opts.host
      , mkt: opts.marketId
      , obfMkt: opts.obfuscatedMarketId
      , aliases: opts.searchAliases
      , fb: issOpts.fallbackFlag
      , isDigitalFeaturesEnabled: issOpts.isDigitalFeaturesEnabled
      , isWayfindingEnabled: issOpts.isWayfindingEnabled
      , issPrimeEligible: issOpts.issPrimeEligible
      , deptText: issOpts.departmentText
      , sugText: issOpts.suggestionText
      , filterAliases: opts.filterAliases
      , cf: issOpts.cf
      , ime: opts.isJpOrCn
      , mktid: opts.marketId
      , qs: opts.isJpOrCn
      , issCorpus: issOpts.issCorpus
      , deepNodeISS: {
          searchAliasAccessor: function($) {
            return (window.SearchPageAccess && window.SearchPageAccess.searchAlias()) ||
                   $('select.searchSelect').children().attr('data-root-alias');
          },
          searchAliasDisplayNameAccessor: function() {
            return (window.SearchPageAccess && window.SearchPageAccess.searchAliasDisplayName());
          }
        }
    };

    // If we aren't using the new ISS then we need to add these properties
    if (!isNewIss) {
      issInitObj.dd = issOpts.dropdown; // The element with id searchDropdownBox doesn't exist in C.
      issInitObj.imeSpacing = issOpts.imeSpacing;
      issInitObj.isNavInline = 1;
      issInitObj.triggerISSOnClick = 0;
      issInitObj.sc = 1;
      issInitObj.np = issOpts.np;
    }

    return issInitObj;
  } // END buildIssInitObject

  
  function logMetrics() {
    if (typeof uet == 'function' && typeof uex == 'function' ) {
      uet('be', 'iss-init-pc', {wb: 1});
      uex('ld', 'iss-init-pc', {wb: 1});
    }
  } // END logMetrics

i.src = window._navbarSpriteUrl;
}(new Image()));

</script><script type='text/template' id='summary-GRID-HERO'>
<~
    // Generates the summary (plain text) of all the selected filters in a filters.
    function generateFilterSummary (filters, attribute, data) {
        if (filters.length > 2) {
            var str = gb.filterController.models[data.eventID].filterPlurals[attribute] || attribute;
            return filters.length + " " + str;
        } else {
            var separator = " " + gb.resources.getString("gb_summary_filter_separator") + " ";
            return _.map(filters, function(filterOption) {
                return data.view.getFilterLabel(filterOption, true);
            }).join(separator);
        }
    }

    // PageData for rendering page number details.
    var pageData = _.find(data.filterOptions, function(filterOption) {
        return filterOption.attribute === "page";
    });

    pageData.dealCount = gb.metadata.getAllDisplayableDealIDs(data.widgetID).length;
    pageData.pageSize  = gb.controller.schedulingParams[data.widgetID].pageSize;

    var selectedFilterTypes = _.filter(data.filterOptions, function(filterOption) {
        return filterOption.selected;
    });

    var filtersByAttr = _.groupBy(selectedFilterTypes, function(filterOption){
        return filterOption.attribute;
    });

    var summary = _.map(filtersByAttr, function(filters, attribute) {
        return {
            attr : attribute,
            text : generateFilterSummary(filters, attribute, data)
        };
    });

    if (pageData.dealCount || summary.length) {
~>
        <span>
<~
            var str;
            var total    = pageData.dealCount;
            var pageSize = pageData.pageSize;
            var start    = (pageData.currentPage - 1) * pageSize + 1;
            var end      = start + pageSize - 1;
                end      = end > total ? total : end;

            if (start > end) { /* Means the pagination has gone too far */
                str = summary.length ? 'gb_no_results_to_show_for' : 'gb_no_results_to_show';
                print(gb.resources.getString(str));
            } else {
                str = summary.length ? 'gb_showing_x_results_for' : 'gb_showing_x_results';
                print(gb.resources.getString(str, {
                    start : start,
                    end   : end,
                    total : total
                }));
            }
~>
        </span>
<~
    }
    if (summary.length) {

        // Sort the items by attribute priority
        summary = _.sortBy(summary, function(item) {
            return _.indexOf(data.attrPriority, item.attr);
        });
        _.each(summary, function(summaryItem, index) {

            // Find the next attributes - ie attributes with lower priority than current.
            // Why? When clicking on any of the links on the breadcrumb, the filtering
            // on the attributes listed after it in the list should be removed.
            var attributes = _.pluck(_.rest(summary, index + 1), 'attr').join(',');
            if (index < summary.length - 1) {
~>
                <span class="a-declarative" data-action="gbfilter-link" data-gbfilter-link="{&quot;linkType&quot;:&quot;clear&quot;,&quot;attributes&quot;:&quot;{{attributes}}&quot;}">
                    <a class="a-link-normal summary" href="#">
<~
            }
~>
                        <span class="a-text-bold">
                            {{summaryItem.text}}
                        </span>
<~
            if (index < summary.length - 1) {
~>
                    </a>
                </span>
<~
            }
~>
            <span class="a-text-bold">
<~
                print(index === summary.length - 1 ? '' : ' : ');
~>
            </span>
<~
        });
~>
        <span class="a-declarative" data-action="gbfilter-clear-all" data-gbfilter-clear-all="{}">
            <a class="a-link-normal a-text-bold" href="#">
                &nbsp;
                <i data-value="{{filtersByAttr}}" class="a-icon a-icon-close a-icon-medium clearFilter"></i>

<script type='text/template' id='pagination-GRID-HERO'>

    var widgetID   = data.widgetID;

<span class="a-declarative" data-action="gbfilter-pagination" data-gbfilter-pagination="{&quot;attribute&quot;:&quot;{{data.attribute}}&quot;,&quot;currentPage&quot;:&quot;{{data.currentPage}}&quot;,&quot;totalPages&quot;:&quot;{{data.totalPages}}&quot;,&quot;widgetID&quot;:&quot;{{widgetID}}&quot;,&quot;filterType&quot;:&quot;pagination&quot;}">

    <div id="pagination-next-{{random}}" class="a-text-center hidden"><ul class="a-pagination"><li class="a-disabled">&larr;<span class="a-letter-space"></span><span class="a-letter-space"></span>{{prevString}}</li> <li class="a-last"><a href="#{{data.dummyUrls.NEXT}}">{{nextString}}<span class="a-letter-space"></span><span class="a-letter-space"></span>&rarr;</a></li></ul></div>

    <div id='pagination-pages-{{random}}'>
<~

        // If only Previous and Next buttons are needed, then do not display the page buttons.
        if(!data.minimalPagination) {

            // We will re-use this var for ellipsis on either sides
            var alreadyPrintedEllipsis = false;
            var pagesToShowOnBothSides = (widgetName === gb.enums.WidgetNames.TAB_HERO || gb.enums.WidgetNames.PC_SUPPLE) ? 1 : 2;

            _.times(data.totalPages, function(i) {
                var index = i + 1;

                if (Math.abs(data.currentPage - index) <= pagesToShowOnBothSides || index === 1 || index === data.totalPages ||
                    (widgetName === gb.enums.WidgetNames.PC_SUPPLE && index === 3 && data.currentPage === 1)) {
                    // Flip so that ellipsis in the other end will be printed if required.
                    alreadyPrintedEllipsis = false;
                    if (index === data.currentPage) {
~>
                        <li class="a-selected"><a href="#">{{index}}</a></li>
<~
                    } else {
                        // Disabling last page number for PC supple widget if it is not among
                        // first 3 pages and the current page is not within last 3 pages.
                        if (widgetName === gb.enums.WidgetNames.PC_SUPPLE &&
                            index === data.totalPages && index > 3 &&
                            data.currentPage < data.totalPages-2) {
~>
                            <li class="a-disabled">{{index}}</li> <~
                        } else { ~>
                            <li data-page="{{index}}" class="a-normal"><a href="#">{{index}}</a></li>
<~
                        }
                    }
                } else if (!alreadyPrintedEllipsis) {
~>
                    <li class="a-disabled">...</li>
<~
                    alreadyPrintedEllipsis = true;
                }
            });
        }

        // Append the page buttons to the proper parent pagination container and
        // hide the other parents.
        _.defer(function($) {

            var parentId;
            if (data.currentPage === 1) {
               parentId = '#pagination-next-' + random;  // show only next button
            } else if(data.currentPage === data.totalPages) {
                parentId = '#pagination-prev-' + random;  // show only prev button
            } else {
                parentId = '#pagination-both-' + random;  // show both buttons
            }

            var prevButton = $('li', parentId).eq(0);
            $('li', '#pagination-pages-' + random).insertAfter(prevButton);
            $(parentId).removeClass('hidden');

        }, gb.Backbone.$);
~>

    </div>

</span>
</script>

</script><script type='text/template' id='summary-GRID-HERO'>
<~
    // Generates the summary (plain text) of all the selected filters in a filters.
    function generateFilterSummary (filters, attribute, data) {
        if (filters.length > 2) {
            var str = gb.filterController.models[data.eventID].filterPlurals[attribute] || attribute;
            return filters.length + " " + str;
        } else {
            var separator = " " + gb.resources.getString("gb_summary_filter_separator") + " ";
            return _.map(filters, function(filterOption) {
                return data.view.getFilterLabel(filterOption, true);
            }).join(separator);
        }
    }

    // PageData for rendering page number details.
    var pageData = _.find(data.filterOptions, function(filterOption) {
        return filterOption.attribute === "page";
    });

    pageData.dealCount = gb.metadata.getAllDisplayableDealIDs(data.widgetID).length;
    pageData.pageSize  = gb.controller.schedulingParams[data.widgetID].pageSize;

    var selectedFilterTypes = _.filter(data.filterOptions, function(filterOption) {
        return filterOption.selected;
    });

    var filtersByAttr = _.groupBy(selectedFilterTypes, function(filterOption){
        return filterOption.attribute;
    });

    var summary = _.map(filtersByAttr, function(filters, attribute) {
        return {
            attr : attribute,
            text : generateFilterSummary(filters, attribute, data)
        };
    });

    if (pageData.dealCount || summary.length) {
~>
        <span>
<~
            var str;
            var total    = pageData.dealCount;
            var pageSize = pageData.pageSize;
            var start    = (pageData.currentPage - 1) * pageSize + 1;
            var end      = start + pageSize - 1;
                end      = end > total ? total : end;

            if (start > end) { /* Means the pagination has gone too far */
                str = summary.length ? 'gb_no_results_to_show_for' : 'gb_no_results_to_show';
                print(gb.resources.getString(str));
            } else {
                str = summary.length ? 'gb_showing_x_results_for' : 'gb_showing_x_results';
                print(gb.resources.getString(str, {
                    start : start,
                    end   : end,
                    total : total
                }));
            }
~>
        </span>
<~
    }
    if (summary.length) {

        // Sort the items by attribute priority
        summary = _.sortBy(summary, function(item) {
            return _.indexOf(data.attrPriority, item.attr);
        });
        _.each(summary, function(summaryItem, index) {

            // Find the next attributes - ie attributes with lower priority than current.
            // Why? When clicking on any of the links on the breadcrumb, the filtering
            // on the attributes listed after it in the list should be removed.
            var attributes = _.pluck(_.rest(summary, index + 1), 'attr').join(',');
            if (index < summary.length - 1) {
~>
                <span class="a-declarative" data-action="gbfilter-link" data-gbfilter-link="{&quot;linkType&quot;:&quot;clear&quot;,&quot;attributes&quot;:&quot;{{attributes}}&quot;}">
                    <a class="a-link-normal summary" href="#">
<~
            }
~>
                        <span class="a-text-bold">
                            {{summaryItem.text}}
                        </span>
<~
            if (index < summary.length - 1) {
~>
                    </a>
                </span>
<~
            }
~>

<script type='text/template' id='pagination-GRID-HERO'>
<~
    var widgetID   = data.widgetID;
    var widgetName = data.widgetName;

    data = data.filterOptions[0];

    // Display pagination bar only if more than one page of data is present.
    if (data.totalPages < 2) {
        return;
    }

    var nextString = gb.resources.getString('gb_next_page');
    var prevString = gb.resources.getString('gb_previous_page');
    var random = Math.random().toString().split('.')[1];
~>

<span class="a-declarative" data-action="gbfilter-pagination" data-gbfilter-pagination="{&quot;attribute&quot;:&quot;{{data.attribute}}&quot;,&quot;currentPage&quot;:&quot;{{data.currentPage}}&quot;,&quot;totalPages&quot;:&quot;{{data.totalPages}}&quot;,&quot;widgetID&quot;:&quot;{{widgetID}}&quot;,&quot;filterType&quot;:&quot;pagination&quot;}">

    <div id="pagination-both-{{random}}" class="a-text-center hidden"><ul class="a-pagination"><li><a href="#{{data.dummyUrls.PREV}}">&larr;<span class="a-letter-space"></span><span class="a-letter-space"></span>{{prevString}}</a></li> <li class="a-last"><a href="#{{data.dummyUrls.NEXT}}">{{nextString}}<span class="a-letter-space"></span><span class="a-letter-space"></span>&rarr;</a></li></ul></div>

    <div id="pagination-next-{{random}}" class="a-text-center hidden"><ul class="a-pagination"><li class="a-disabled">&larr;<span class="a-letter-space"></span><span class="a-letter-space"></span>{{prevString}}</li> <li class="a-last"><a href="#{{data.dummyUrls.NEXT}}">{{nextString}}<span class="a-letter-space"></span><span class="a-letter-space"></span>&rarr;</a></li></ul></div>

    <div id="pagination-prev-{{random}}" class="a-text-center hidden"><ul class="a-pagination"><li><a href="#{{data.dummyUrls.PREV}}">&larr;<span class="a-letter-space"></span><span class="a-letter-space"></span>{{prevString}}</a></li> <li class="a-disabled a-last">{{nextString}}<span class="a-letter-space"></span><span class="a-letter-space"></span>&rarr;</li></ul></div>

    <div id='pagination-pages-{{random}}'>
<~

        // If only Previous and Next buttons are needed, then do not display the page buttons.
        if(!data.minimalPagination) {

            // We will re-use this var for ellipsis on either sides
            var alreadyPrintedEllipsis = false;
            var pagesToShowOnBothSides = (widgetName === gb.enums.WidgetNames.TAB_HERO || gb.enums.WidgetNames.PC_SUPPLE) ? 1 : 2;

            _.times(data.totalPages, function(i) {
                var index = i + 1;

                if (Math.abs(data.currentPage - index) <= pagesToShowOnBothSides || index === 1 || index === data.totalPages ||
                    (widgetName === gb.enums.WidgetNames.PC_SUPPLE && index === 3 && data.currentPage === 1)) {
                    // Flip so that ellipsis in the other end will be printed if required.
                    alreadyPrintedEllipsis = false;
                    if (index === data.currentPage) {
~>
                        <li class="a-selected"><a href="#">{{index}}</a></li>
<~
                    } else {
                        // Disabling last page number for PC supple widget if it is not among
                        // first 3 pages and the current page is not within last 3 pages.
                        if (widgetName === gb.enums.WidgetNames.PC_SUPPLE &&
                            index === data.totalPages && index > 3 &&
                            data.currentPage < data.totalPages-2) {
~>
                            <li class="a-disabled">{{index}}</li> <~
                        } else { ~>
                            <li data-page="{{index}}" class="a-normal"><a href="#">{{index}}</a></li>
<~
                        }
                    }
                } else if (!alreadyPrintedEllipsis) {
~>
                    <li class="a-disabled">...</li>
<~
                    alreadyPrintedEllipsis = true;
                }
            });
        }

        // Append the page buttons to the proper parent pagination container and
        // hide the other parents.
        _.defer(function($) {

            var parentId;
            if (data.currentPage === 1) {
               parentId = '#pagination-next-' + random;  // show only next button
            } else if(data.currentPage === data.totalPages) {
                parentId = '#pagination-prev-' + random;  // show only prev button
            } else {
                parentId = '#pagination-both-' + random;  // show both buttons
            }

            var prevButton = $('li', parentId).eq(0);
            $('li', '#pagination-pages-' + random).insertAfter(prevButton);
            $(parentId).removeClass('hidden');

        }, gb.Backbone.$);
~>

    </div>

</span>
</script>

</script><script type="text/template" id="title-SUPPLE">
<~
    var title             = data.deal.detail.title;
    var url               = data.getReffedURL(data.deal.detail.URL, gb.metrics.refTags.title);
    var showShortCellView = gb.controller.schedulingParams[data.widgetID].showShortCellView;
    var cssClass          = 'dealTitleOneLine unitLineHeight ';
    var itemType          = data.deal.detail.itemType;
    var titleColorBase    = 'base';
    var titleColorLink    = 'link';
    var cssClassBase      = 'restVisible ';
    var cssClassLink      = 'hoverVisible ';
    var baseVisiblity     = '';
    var widthCSS          = '';
    if(!showShortCellView){
        cssClassBase      = 'hoverVisible ';
        cssClassLink      = 'restVisible ';
    }

    if(data.deal.dealType === gb.enums.DealTypes.BD && itemType != gb.enums.ItemTypes.SINGLE) {
        cssClass = 'dealTitleThreeLine ';
    } else if( (!showShortCellView && data.deal.dealType != gb.enums.DealTypes.DOTD) ||
        (data.deal.dealType === gb.enums.DealTypes.LOCAL) ||
        (data.deal.dealType === gb.enums.DealTypes.DOTD  && !data.isDoubleCell && !showShortCellView)) {
        cssClass = 'dealTitleTwoLine ';
    }

    if( (data.deal.dealType === gb.enums.DealTypes.DOTD && (itemType != gb.enums.ItemTypes.SINGLE || data.isDoubleCell)) ||
        (data.deal.dealType === gb.enums.DealTypes.LOCAL) ||
        (data.deal.dealType === gb.enums.DealTypes.BD && itemType != gb.enums.ItemTypes.SINGLE) ) {
        baseVisiblity   = 'visibleCss ';
    }
    else {
        baseVisiblity   = 'hiddenCss ';
    }

    if(data.deal.auxiliaryData.breaksMAP) {
        baseVisiblity   = 'visibleCss ';
        cssClass = 'dealTitleTwoLine ';
    }

    if(data.deal.dealState === gb.enums.DealStates.SOLDOUT || data.deal.dealState === gb.enums.DealStates.EXPIRED || data.deal.dealState === gb.enums.DealStates.WAITLISTFULL) {
        titleColorBase = 'secondary ';
        titleColorLink = 'secondary ';
    }
    if(data.deal.dealType === gb.enums.DealTypes.DOTD && data.isDoubleCell){
        widthCSS = 'doubleCellTitle';
    } else {
        widthCSS = 'singleCellTitle';
    }

    var cssStringBase = cssClass + cssClassBase + baseVisiblity + widthCSS;
    var cssStringLink = cssClass + cssClassLink + widthCSS;

    if(data.deal.dealState === gb.enums.DealStates.UPCOMING || data.deal.dealState === gb.enums.DealStates.COMINGSOON) {
        if(data.deal.teaser.teaserLine) {
            title = data.deal.teaser.teaserLine;
        }
        if(data.deal.teaser.teaserURL) {
            url = data.deal.teaser.teaserURL;
        } else {
            url = "";
        }
    }
    if(title === null || title === undefined) {
        title = '';
    }
    if(url) {
        url = data.getReffedURL(url, gb.metrics.refTags.title);

<script type="text/JavaScript">
(function () {
    "use strict";

    var P = (window.AmazonUIPageJS ? AmazonUIPageJS : window.P);

    var enableYBHLink = function() {
        P.when('p13n-sc-jQuery').execute(function($) {
            $("#ybh-link").click(function() {
                $.ajax({
                      url: '/gp/recent-history-footer/external/ybh-handler.html/277-0007204-4414934',
                      type: "POST",
                      timeout: 2000,
                      data: {
                           parentSession    : '277-0007204-4414934',
                           relatedRequestId : '1GKBNABFA6E99R7X05DV',
                           currentPageType  : 'GoldBox'
                      },
                      dataType: "text",
                      success: function (data, status) {
                           $("#ybh-link").hide();
                           $("#ybh-text-off").hide();
                           $("#ybh-text-on").show();
                      }
                });
            });
        });
    };

    var lazyLoadRHF = function($) {
        var loadCarousel = function(html) {
            P.when('p13n-sc-carousel-init', 'rhf-container')
             .execute(function(carouselInitializer, rhfContainer) {
                rhfContainer.html(html);
                carouselInitializer.init(rhfContainer);
                enableYBHLink();
            });
        };

        var handleSuccess = function(data) {
            if (typeof(data) === 'object' && data.success && data.html) {
                loadCarousel(data.html);
            } else {
                handleError();
            }
        };

        var handleError = function() {
            P.when('rhf-container', 'rhf-error')
             .execute(function(rhfContainer, rhfError) {
                rhfContainer.hide();
                rhfError.show();
            });
        };

        $.ajax({
            url: '/gp/recent-history-footer/external/rhf-handler.html/277-0007204-4414934',
            type: "POST",
            timeout: 5000,
            data: {
                             isAUI : (typeof window.P === 'object' && window.P.AUI_BUILD_DATE) ? 1 : 0,
                     parentSession : '277-0007204-4414934',
                  relatedRequestId : '1GKBNABFA6E99R7X05DV',
                   currentPageType : 'GoldBox',
                currentSubPageType : 'main',
                       excludeASIN : '',
                          auiDebug : '',
                          rviAsins : '',
                          rhfState : '',
                          rhfAsins : '',
                       noP13NCache : '',
                         recsAsins : '',
                        customerID : '',
                   testRecsFailure : '',
                    weblabTriggers : '',
           contextMetadataOverride : ''
            },
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (data, status) {
                handleSuccess(data);
            },
            error: function (xhr, status) {
                handleError();
            }
        });
    };

    P.when('p13n-sc-jQuery').execute(function($) {
        P.declare('rhf-container', $("#rhf-container"));
        P.declare('rhf-error', $("#rhf-error"));
        P.declare('rhf-frame', $(".rhf-frame"));
    });

    P.when('p13n-sc-jQuery', 'rhf-container', 'rhf-frame',
            'p13n-sc-call-on-visible', 'p13n-sc-carousel-init')
     .execute(function($, rhfContainer, rhfFrame, callOnVisible, carouselInitializer) {
        rhfFrame.show();
        callOnVisible.register(rhfContainer, function () { lazyLoadRHF($); }, { distance: '-400' })
    });

})();
</script>
